<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>COSTCO WHOLESALE CORPORATION REPORTS SECOND QUARTER AND
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">YEAR-TO-DATE</FONT></FONT> </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>OPERATING RESULTS FOR FISCAL 2020 AND
FEBRUARY SALES RESULTS </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">ISSAQUAH, Wash., March&nbsp;5, 2020 - Costco Wholesale Corporation (&#147;Costco&#148; or the &#147;Company&#148;) (Nasdaq:
COST) today announced its operating results for the second quarter (twelve weeks) and the first 24 weeks of fiscal 2020, ended February&nbsp;16, 2020. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net sales for the quarter increased 10.5&nbsp;percent, to $38.26&nbsp;billion from $34.63&nbsp;billion last year. Net sales for the first 24 weeks increased
8.1&nbsp;percent, to $74.49&nbsp;billion from $68.94&nbsp;billion last year. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Comparable sales for the second quarter fiscal 2020 were as follows: </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Excluding the impacts from changes in gasoline prices and foreign exchange. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Due to Thanksgiving occurring a week later this year, for the quarter: total and comparable sales were positively impacted by approximately <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-half</FONT> percent; and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">e-commerce</FONT> sales were positively impacted by an estimated 11 percentage points. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Reported net income for the quarter was $931&nbsp;million, or $2.10 per diluted share, compared to $889&nbsp;million, or $2.01 per diluted share, last year.
Net income for the first 24 weeks was $1.77&nbsp;billion, or $4.00 per diluted share, compared to $1.66&nbsp;billion, or $3.74 per diluted share, last year. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the four-week reporting month of February, ended March&nbsp;1, 2020, the Company reported net sales of $12.20&nbsp;billion, an increase of
13.8&nbsp;percent from $10.72&nbsp;billion last year. For the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">twenty-six</FONT> week period ended March&nbsp;1, 2020, net sales were $80.76&nbsp;billion, an increase of 8.5&nbsp;percent from $74.42&nbsp;billion last
year. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Comparable sales for the February and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-date</FONT></FONT> periods ended
March&nbsp;1, 2020, were as follows: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="line-height:3.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:3.00pt solid #000000">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">February sales
benefited from an uptick in consumer demand in the fourth week of the reporting period. We attribute this to concerns over the Coronavirus and estimate the positive impact on total and comparable sales to be approximately three percent. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Costco currently operates 785 warehouses, including 546 in the United States and Puerto Rico, 100 in Canada, 39 in Mexico, 29 in the United Kingdom, 26 in
Japan, 16 in Korea, 13 in Taiwan, 11 in Australia, two in Spain, and one each in Iceland, France, and China. Costco also operates <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">e-commerce</FONT> sites in the U.S., Canada, the United Kingdom, Mexico, Korea,
Taiwan, Japan, and Australia. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">A conference call to discuss these results is scheduled for 2:00 p.m. (PT) today, March&nbsp;5, 2020, and is available via
a webcast on www.costco.com (click on Investor Relations and &#147;Play Webcast&#148;). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Certain statements contained in this document and the <FONT

var Show={};Show.LastAR=null,Show.showAR=function(a,r,w){if(Show.LastAR)Show.hideAR();var e=a;while(e&&e.nodeName!='TABLE')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e||e.nodeName!='TABLE'){var ref=((window)?w.document:document).getElementById(r);if(ref){e=ref.cloneNode(!0);
e.removeAttribute('id');a.parentNode.appendChild(e)}}
if(e)e.style.display='block';Show.LastAR=e};Show.hideAR=function(){Show.LastAR.style.display='none'};Show.toggleNext=function(a){var e=a;while(e.nodeName!='DIV')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e.style){}else if(!e.style.display){}else{var d,p_;if(e.style.display=='none'){d='block';p='-'}else{d='none';p='+'}
e.style.display=d;if(a.textContent){a.textContent=p+a.textContent.substring(1)}else{a.innerText=p+a.innerText.substring(1)}}}
